if (!is_file('TODO')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: TODO');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('TODO')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != '368c9de5682701e653e58e792f240de37d2db110') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '368c9de5682701e653e58e792f240de37d2db110') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'e6eefa5c7e492edf41b2b2396141bf65169cefdb') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '368c9de5682701e653e58e792f240de37d2db110') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('doc/faq.md')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: doc/faq.md');
	writefile_4();
	if (!is_file('doc/faq.md')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): doc/faq.md');
	} else if (sha1_file('doc/faq.md') != 'fb16342461eb0985f113bb7b479003c4ddb741de') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): doc/faq.md');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('doc/faq.md', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of doc/faq.md');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('doc/faq.md') !== 'fb16342461eb0985f113bb7b479003c4ddb741de') {
		if (@sha1_file('doc/faq.md') !== 'e03e56f7bb3fe23c17514669432288899ab5f814') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: doc/faq.md');
			$tmp = pathinfo('doc/faq.md');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('doc/faq.md')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('doc/faq.md', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('doc/faq.md') !== 'fb16342461eb0985f113bb7b479003c4ddb741de') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): doc/faq.md');
		}
	}
}

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') != '6dde545c0ad866dca77e2c27b2d38d6209ac60e9') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');

	}

	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '6dde545c0ad866dca77e2c27b2d38d6209ac60e9') {

			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}

		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '6dde545c0ad866dca77e2c27b2d38d6209ac60e9') {
